Our Privacy and Security Policy (the "Privacy Policy") is intended to inform you about the collection and use of your personal data when using our websites and provide you with a safe and secure experience in fashion, style and shopping.</p>\r\n                <p class="pb_20">This Cookies Policy went into effect on the date noted above, but please be aware that we reserve the right to review and update this Cookie Policy from time to time. Don\xe2\x80\x99t worry, if we make any material changes to the Cookie Policy, we will notify you by means of a general notice on the sites prior to the change taking effect. </p>\r\n                <p class="t_bold">What Are Cookies?</p>\r\n                <p class="pb_20">Cookies are small text files that are stored on your computer or device when you visit our sites. Cookies allow a website to recognise a particular device or browser. The use of cookies is a standard practice among websites to collect information about visitors\xe2\x80\x99 activities and to make using websites easier for you.</p>\r\n                <p class="t_bold">How Do We Use Cookies?</p>\r\n                <p class="pb_20">There are different types of cookies used for different purposes, such as functionality, analytics, customer preference, or for marketing purposes. Here is the breakdown of each: </p>\r\n                <ol class="number">\r\n                    <li class="pb_10">Functionality cookies: these cookies allow you to navigate the site and use our features, such as keeping items in your basket when shopping online. These cookies expire when the browser is closed.</li>\r\n                    <li class="pb_10">Analytics cookies: we partner with third parties, such as Google Analytics, to gather information about your activities on this site and other sites over time for non-advertising purposes such as improving the site functionality and website experience. To learn more about how Google Analytics collects and processes data and the choices Google may offer to control these activities, you may visit http://www.google.com/intl/en/policies/privacy/partners/. </li>\r\n                    <li class="pb_10">Preference cookies: we use these cookies to help us remember your preferences, such as language or location, to enhance your shipping experience. </li>\r\n                    <li class="pb_10">Advertising or targeting cookies: We partner with third parties that may use technologies such as cookies to gather information about your activities on this and sites other websites in order to provide you with relevant advertising based upon your browsing activities and interests. This type of advertising is sometimes called interest-based advertising. No personally-identifiable information is collected or used in this process.</li>\r\n                </ol>\r\n                <p class="t_bold">How Do I Opt Out Of Cookies?</p>\r\n                <ul class="circle pa_20 pt_10 pb_20">\r\n                    <li>If you wish to not have cookies that are used for interest-based advertising, you may <a class="underline" href="http://preferences-mgr.truste.com/?pid=truste01&aid=preference_manager01&type=public ">opt-out by clicking here</a> for partners that participate in the TRUSTe opt-out tool (or <a class="underline" href="http://www.youronlinechoices.eu">if located in the European Union click here</a>). If you wish to opt-out from this type of advertising for <a class="underline" href="http://www.networkadvertising.org/choices/#completed ">companies that participate in the Network Advertising Initiative, please click here</a>. If you wish <a class="underline" href="http://www.aboutads.info/choices/ ">to opt-out from this type of advertising for companies that participate in the Digital Advertising Alliance (\xe2\x80\x9cDAA\xe2\x80\x9d), you can do so here</a>. Please note that this does not opt you out of being served ads. You will continue to receive generic ads. Forever 21 adheres to the DAA\xe2\x80\x99s Self-Regulatory Principles.</li>\r\n                    <li>You can opt out of the Google Analytics Advertising Features we use by indicating your preference using the interest-based <a href="http://www.networkadvertising.org/choices/ ">opt-out link here</a>. Google also provides a complete privacy policy, and <a href="https://tools.google.com/dlpage/gaoptout/">instructions on opting out of Google Analytics here</a>. Note that Google\xe2\x80\x99s opt-out mechanism is specific to Google activities and does not affect the activities of other ad networks or analytics providers that we may use.</li>\r\n                    <li><span class="t_bold">"Do Not Track" Technology:</span> Some newer web browsers have a "Do Not Track" preference that transmits a "Do Not Track" header to the websites you visit with information indicating that you do not want your activity to be tracked. We currently do not respond to browser "Do Not Track" signals.</li>\r\n                </ul>\r\n                <p class="pb_20">Lastly, to manage the cookies that are placed on your computer, you may configure your internet browser to refuse, accept or delete cookies from our sites at any time. Some of the cookies we use may be more persistent in nature. These persistent cookies may not be deleted when other cookies are deleted. Please check your browser and browser settings to determine where these types of cookies are stored and whether and how they may be deleted. The help portion of the toolbar on most browsers will tell you how to prevent your browser from accepting new cookies, how to have the browser notify you when you receive a new cookie, or how to disable most cookies altogether. Please note that if cookies are disabled or removed, not all features of our sites will operate as intended.</p>\r\n                <p class="t_bold">Why does this matter?</p>\r\n                <p class="pb_10">By using our site, you agree to us placing these sorts of cookies on your device and accessing them when you visit the site in the future. If you want to delete any cookies that are already on your computer, the \xe2\x80\x9cOpt Out\xe2\x80\x9d section above can provide you with more information.</p>\r\n                <p class="pb_10">Further information about cookies can be found at https://ico.org.uk/for-organisations/guide-to-pecr/cookies-and-similar-technologies/. As mentioned before, it\xe2\x80\x99s important to note that by deleting or disabling future cookies, your user experience may be affected and you might not be able to take advantage of certain functions of our site.</p>\r\n            </div>\r\n            <!-- Content Container E -->\r\n        </div>\r\n    </div>\r\n</div>\r\n    <!-- Cookies Popup E-->\r\n    <!-- Privacy Popup S-->\r\n    <div id="privacy" class="flex-modal-hide long">\r\n    <div class="fc col_s_10_of_10 col_m_8_of_12 col_l_8_of_16">\r\n        <button class="quick_close" type="button"></button>\r\n        <div class="container row pa_20">\r\n            <div class="p_title"><strong>Privacy Policy</strong></div>\r\n            <div class="ws_100 txl pt_10 r_content">\r\n                <span class="t_small pb_10">(Effective Date: May 16, 2018)</span>\r\n\r\n                <p class="pb_20">Forever 21, Inc., 3880 N. Cookies allow a website to recognize a particular device or browser. The use of cookies is a standard practice among websites to collect information about visitors\xe2\x80\x99 activities while using the website.\r\n                    </li>\r\n                    <li>\r\n                        <span class="t_bold">Beacons</span>\r\n                        is programming code that is designed to collect information about your interactions with the Site, such as the links you click on. Various browsers may offer their own management tools for removing local shared objects.
